### Winggarden Air Tree ###

shared_focus = {
	id = WIN_chiropterran_fighters
	icon = GFX_goal_POL_recon_aircraft
	x = -4
	y = 1
	relative_position_id = WIN_the_establishment
	cost = 4.40
	prerequisite = { 
	    focus = WIN_the_establishment 
	}

	ai_will_do = {
		factor = 5
	}
	completion_reward = {
		log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: Focus WIN_chiropterran_fighters"
		custom_effect_tooltip = WIN_decrease_1_half_w_increase_3_c_decrease_1_half_ct_tp
		add_doctrine_cost_reduction = {
			name = air_doc_bonus
			cost_reduction = 0.5
			uses = 2
			category = air_doctrine
		}

		add_tech_bonus = {
			name = early_fighter
			bonus = 1.0
			uses = 1
			category = light_fighter
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_dlc = "By Blood Alone" }
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_tech = advanced_small_airframe
					has_tech = engines_4
					has_tech = aa_hmg
				}

				create_equipment_variant = {
					name = "Advanced Fighter"
					type = small_plane_airframe_3
					modules = {
						fixed_main_weapon_slot = heavy_mg_2x
						engine_type_slot = engine_4_1x
						special_type_slot_1 = lmg_defense_turret
					}
					icon = "GFX_BAT_fighter3_medium"
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = small_plane_airframe_3
					amount = 100
					producer = WIN
					variant_name = "Advanced Fighter"
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_tech = improved_small_airframe
					has_tech = engines_3
					has_tech = aa_hmg
				}

				create_equipment_variant = {
					name = "Improved Fighter"
					type = small_plane_airframe_2
					modules = {
						fixed_main_weapon_slot = heavy_mg_2x
						engine_type_slot = engine_3_1x
						special_type_slot_1 = lmg_defense_turret
					}
					icon = "GFX_BAT_fighter2_medium"
				}
				add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
					type = small_plane_airframe_2
					amount = 100
					producer = WIN

				}
			}
			HIP = {

			}
		}

            target = HIP
            type = annex_everything
		}
	}
	search_filters = { 
		FOCUS_FILTER_ANNEXATION
	}
}

		    limit = {
			    has_idea = WIN_the_open_door_policy_idea_3
			}
			swap_ideas = {
			    remove_idea = WIN_the_open_door_policy_idea_3
				add_idea = WIN_the_open_door_policy_idea_4
			}
		}
		else = {
		    add_ideas = WIN_the_open_door_policy_idea
		}
		add_stability = 0.03
		add_war_support = 0.03
		every_owned_state = {
			limit = { 
			    is_core_of = ROOT 
			}
			add_extra_state_shared_building_slots = 1
			add_manpower = 10000
		}
	}
	search_filters = { 
		FOCUS_FILTER_POLITICAL
		FOCUS_FILTER_STABILITY
		FOCUS_FILTER_WAR_SUPPORT
		FOCUS_FILTER_MANPOWER
		FOCUS_FILTER_INDUSTRY
	}
}
